***gooien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gooien.html>gooien</a> (1377)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">goyen</i>, further etymology debated. Possibly from an ancestor of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gauw.html>gauw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quickly, soon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, although other origins have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> suggested.
</p>

</p>

***gook.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gook.html>gook</a> (69804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> used by <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a>.S. Marines in the early 20th century;<sup id="cite_ref-Dictionary.com_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Dictionary.com-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Pearson_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Pearson-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> the earliest written example <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dated 1920.<sup id="cite_ref-Seligman_3-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Seligman-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p><p>Folk etymology suggests that during the Korean War, young Korean children would point at <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a>.S. <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a> and shout in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Korean_language" class="extiw" title="w:Korean language">Korean</a></span> <i class="Kore mention" lang="ko">美國</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ko-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Miguk</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">America</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>Soldiers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> the word as “me gook”, as if the children <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> defining themselves as “gooks”. The <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a> proceeded to use that term to refer to the Koreans. The word <span lang="ko" class="Kore">국</span> (<span lang="ko" class="Kore">國</span>, <span lang="ko-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">guk</span>) itself simply means “country”. This explanation ignores the fact that there are many examples of the word's use that pre-date the Korean War.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gook.html>gook</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gooks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ethnic slur</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person of Far Eastern or Oceanian descent, especially a Vietnamese, Filipino, Chinese, Japanese or Korean person.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A Vietnamese insurgent in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vietnam_War" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>, particularly a member of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Viet_Cong" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Viet Cong">Viet Cong</a>.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A foreigner, especially an enemy soldier in wartime.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rhodesia" class="extiw" title="w:Rhodesia">Rhodesia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A black insurgent in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rhodesian_Bush_War" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Rhodesian Bush War">Rhodesian Bush War</a>.
<ul><li><b>1997</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a> Gledhill, <i>One <a href = vnd.unilang:commando.html>Commando</a>: Rhodesia's Last Years amp; the <a href = vnd.unilang:guerilla.html>Guerilla</a> War it Never <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a></i>, p. 55:
<dl><dd>"But <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> do a <a href = vnd.unilang:fucking.html>fucking</a> good job of it. Jesus, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> slew long <b>gooks</b> this last trip," quipped Mark.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In the US, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gook.html>gook</a></b> refers especially to a Vietnamese person in the context of the Vietnam War, and particularly to the Viet Cong. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally considered to be highly offensive, on par with nigger.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gookland</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possible blend of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">goop</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gunk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gook.html>gook</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gooks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:grime.html>Grime</a> or mud.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1983</b>,  Len <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Connor,  <cite>A Reporter in Sweet Chicago</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=mGArAAAAMAAJ">[1]</a></sup>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 351:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Roost No More" <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a yellow <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gook.html>gook</a></b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a>'s people would spread around, for a fee, on the ledges of <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a> and commercial buildings plagued by pigeons.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:goor.html>goor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">filthy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:goor.html>goor</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gore.html>gore</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud; dirt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gurą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">manure; filth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷʰer-</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gordel.html>gordel</a> (4923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gorden.html>gorden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gurden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gurdijaną</i>.

***goth.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a> (92842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>Goth</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">person of a Germanic culture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Gothic</i> describing a black horror novel.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">goths</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A punk-derived subculture of people who predominantly dress in black, associated with mournful music and <a href = vnd.unilang:attitudes.html>attitudes</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MC_Frontalot" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:MC Frontalot">MC Frontalot</a> (music),  “Goth Girls”, in  <cite>Nerdcore <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>Rising</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://frontalot.com/index.php/?page=lyricsamp;lyricid=14">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>I think that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a></b> could flower in nerdcore's embrace.</dd>
<dd>I converted Edward Gorey's lettering into a typeface,</dd>
<dd>befriended vampires on LJ and <a href = vnd.unilang:myspace.html>Myspace</a>,</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> put that spooky echo filter on the bass<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> into <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a></b> for many years.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A style of punk rock influenced by glam rock; gothic rock.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> part of the <a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a> subculture.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> saw a solitary <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a></b> hanging out on the <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a> of the train station.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Relating to this music or these people.
<dl><dd><i>With her black <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> and dyed hair, Melanie looked very <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a></b> compared to her classmates.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2014</b>, Michelle Madow, <i>The Secret Diamond <a href = vnd.unilang:sisters.html>Sisters</a></i> (page 39)
<dl><dd>One of them looked like a total <a href = vnd.unilang:freak.html>freak</a> who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> come straight off a <a href = vnd.unilang:cirque.html>Cirque</a> du <a href = vnd.unilang:soleil.html>Soleil</a> stage, with blue streaks in her hair, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>goth</a></b> bracelets up her arm and so much black <a href = vnd.unilang:eyeliner.html>eyeliner</a> that she could be on the set of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:cleopatra.html>Cleopatra</a></i>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***goudkoorts.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goudkoorts.html>goudkoorts</a> (49430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goud.html>goud</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koorts.html>koorts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fever, disease</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goudkoorts.html>goudkoorts</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goudkoorts.html>goudkoortsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***gouw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gouw.html>gouw</a> (29291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gou</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gau</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gō</i> (genitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gooy</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gawją</i>, a collective form equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a prefix that indicates a single collective whole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ouwe.html>ouwe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> near water or drenched with water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">gea</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:goa.html>goa</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gau</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gouw.html>gouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gouw.html>gouwen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gouw.html>gouwtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">gouwken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> geographical area; shire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Dietse <a href = vnd.unilang:gouw.html>gouwen</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">in the Low Countries</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***graad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:graad.html>graad</a> (9240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">graet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gradus</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:graag.html>graag</a> (204)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gradig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">desirous, willing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grādag</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">desirous, hungry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grēdagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hungry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***gracht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>gracht</a> (19416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>gracht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*graft</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*graht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*graftuz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Amsterdam_Zentrum_20091106_075.JPG/220px-Amsterdam_Zentrum_20091106_075.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Amsterdam_Zentrum_20091106_075.JPG/330px-Amsterdam_Zentrum_20091106_075.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Amsterdam_Zentrum_20091106_075.JPG/440px-Amsterdam_Zentrum_20091106_075.JPG 2x" data-file-width="4272" data-file-height="2848" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>gracht</a></b> in Amsterdam.</i><br />A <b>canal</b> in Amsterdam.</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>gracht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grachten.html>grachten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>grachtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ditch</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">trench</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in the countryside, referring to both those that contain water and those that are dry</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2017</b> January 10, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>Laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>Nieuws</a></i>, "Monsterfile <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> E17 <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeval.html>ongeval</a> in Destelbergen, <a href = vnd.unilang:vrachtwagen.html>vrachtwagen</a> in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gracht.html>gracht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> E40".

This caused the <a href = vnd.unilang:truck.html>truck</a>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> loaded with earth, to end up on its side in the <b>ditch</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

***graf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:graf.html>graf</a> (1812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:graf.html>graf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grabą</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grabō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grave, trench, ditch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graf.html>graf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graven.html>graven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graf.html>grafje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">grave</span></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">familiegraf</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">grafgift</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">grafmongool</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grafsteen.html>grafsteen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">graftak</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:massagraf.html>massagraf</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graven.html>graven</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grave</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">serious, grave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Most likely influenced by Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a></i> which can mean "serious, grave" as well as "very". The alternative form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graaf.html>graaf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">very</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the same origin and meaning, but stays <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> to the original French pronunciation.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graf.html>graf</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> very
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:graf.html>graf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duur.html>duur</a></i>  |  That's very expensive</dd></dl></li></ol>

***graffiti.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a> (16261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Drawings or <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> drawn on a surface in a public place, usually made without authorization.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaeology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Informal inscriptions, figure drawings, etc., as opposed to official inscriptions.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no universal singular form to denote a single piece of <a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a>. In archaeology, and occasionally elsewhere, graffito <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used, reflecting the Italian singular. There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> some non-standard usage of graffitus, as though it <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> Latin (compare focus, plural foci); graffitum, also Latin sounding (though this would technically form the plural <i>*graffita</i>; cf. millennium, plural <a href = vnd.unilang:millennia.html>millennia</a>); and <a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a> itself, unmodified.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaeology</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cave painting</span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en">epigraphy</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">graffitis</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">graffitiing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">graffitied</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To mark a surface with such images.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:graffiti.html>graffiti</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:viltstift.html>viltstift</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:spuitbus.html>spuitbus</a> aangebrachte <a href = vnd.unilang:figuren.html>figuren</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:teksten.html>teksten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muren.html>muren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enz.html>enz</a></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Gramophone</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a trademark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emile_Berliner" class="extiw" title="w:Emile Berliner">Emile <a href = vnd.unilang:berliner.html>Berliner</a></a> after the invention of the first <span class="Latn" lang="en">phonograph</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γράμμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grámma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">letter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φωνή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phōnḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***gramschap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gramschap.html>gramschap</a> (60842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gramschap.html>gramschap</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gram</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-schap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gramschap.html>gramschap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic or dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ire, anger, wrath
<ul><li>Dorothée Sturkenboom, <i>Spectators <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hartstocht.html>hartstocht</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:sekse.html>sekse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:emotionele.html>emotionele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cultuur.html>cultuur</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achttiende.html>achttiende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a></i>, 1998, 103.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> spectatoriale <a href = vnd.unilang:gedachtegoed.html>gedachtegoed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toorn.html>toorn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> in the spectators <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gramschap.html>gramschap</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:genoemd.html>genoemd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nauw.html>nauw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwant.html>verwant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> wraakzucht <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haat.html>haat</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the belief system of the spectator papers, wrath <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> often also called <b>ire</b> in the spectator publications <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> closely related to vindictiveness and hatred.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***granaat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a> (7372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">garnate</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grenate</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">grenat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pomus granatus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seeded apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaten.html>granaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A grenade; e.g. a hand grenade, an artillery shell.</li>
<li>A garnet.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">granaatsteen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pomegranate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fruit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The pomegranate plant, <i>Punica granatum</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">granaatappelboom</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***granaatappel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappel</a> (92814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">garnate-appel</i>, also in phrases like <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:appelen.html>appelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> gernaten</i>. A partial loan-translation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">pume grenate</i>, also found as simply <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">grenate</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaat.html>granaat</a></i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappels.html>granaatappels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">granaatappelen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:granaatappel.html>granaatappeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">granaatappelke</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The fruit pomegranate.</li>
<li>The plant Punica granatum, which produces it.</li></ol>
